================================================================================

Many labels have PDS3 syntax errors related to missing quotes around "N/A".

Many quoted values of N/A have an extraneous leading space: " N/A".

Some VIMS labels have multi-line comments, where "/*" appears on one line but
"*/" appears on a later line. This is invalid syntax.

Volume COVIMS_0001 is lacking in a "label" subdirectory, which contains the
referenced .FMT files in the labels. The later volumes do contain this
subdirectory.

Label file COVIMS_0024/data/2008017T190718_2008017T201544/v1579292302_1.lbl
incorrectly refers to data file v1579292302.qub:
  ^HEADER                          = ("v1579292302.qub", 1)
  ^HISTORY                         = ("v1579292302.qub", 22)
  ^QUBE                            = ("v1579292302.qub", 47)
The correct filename is v1579292302_1.qub

Volume COVIMS_0003 has a data subdirectory incorrectly named
1866163T033548_2002199T111000.

================================================================================

https://github.com/SETI/pds-webserver/issues/21

START_TIME and STOP_TIME are backwards in many COVIMS observations. This affects
251 observations. In OPUS we set the stop time equal to the start time.

================================================================================

https://github.com/SETI/pds-webserver/issues/21
https://github.com/SETI/pds-opus/issues/336

SPACECRAFT_CLOCK_START/STOP_COUNT have invalid suffixes in 2 COVIMS
observations. In OPUS we set them to .000.

We are replacing SCLK .971 and .973 with .000 for lack of anything better to do.

2018-08-23 02:14:27 | pds.opus_import.main |--| ERROR | [COVIMS_0017 index row 422] Unable to parse Cassini SCLK "1/1550584847.971": Cassini clock trailing field out of range 0-255: 1550584847.971
2018-08-23 02:15:21 | pds.opus_import.main |--| ERROR | [COVIMS_0017 index row 1555] Unable to parse Cassini SCLK "1/1551973665.973": Cassini clock trailing field out of range 0-255: 1551973665.973

================================================================================

https://github.com/SETI/pds-opus/issues/329

SPACECRAFT_CLOCK_STOP_COUNT has an illegal value in the index. It has been fixed
in the metadata index.

COVIMS_0029_index.tab line 398:

2018-06-16 18:43:27 | pds.opus_import.main |--| ERROR | Column "spacecraft_clock_count2" in table "obs_mission_cassini" has minimum value 1280000000.0 but 90193967
1.145 is too small [line 398]

================================================================================

https://github.com/SETI/pds-opus/issues/328, etc.

COVIMS index files use -999, -1.E32 and +1.E32 to indicate unknown/missing/invalid
values in many columns of the index files, but these constants are never defined
in the labels. We have fixed this in our own metadata files.

================================================================================

The following files are corrupt. In many cases, this was caused by a overflow in the ISIS2 header,
which caused the data array to begin at an incorrect byte offset. In every case, we were able to
repair the file.

================================================================================

This Python data structure handles duplicated data files. These are files that have different PDS3
version numbers but the same clock count. Some of these are missing the initial "v" in the filename.
In most cases, the file with the highest version number is the only one that should have been
archived. However, there are exceptions, where the highest version number is not the preferred one.

Note that the last data directory on COVIMS_0012 contains files that are duplicated on COVIMS_0013.
The files should not have appeared on COVIMS_0012, but are identical to those re-delivered on
COVIMS_0013.

# (pds4_name, label_tag, data_tag, pds3_path)
#
# pds4_name = PDS4 filename without directory path or extension
# label_tag = "1.0" for best, "PRE" if marked "preliminary", "OLD" if creation date is earlier,
#             "DUP" if identical, "NOV" if the source file is missing the leading "v".
# data_tag = "SAME" if the same, "DIFF" if different, "----" for selected version.

VERSIONS = [
